adds a block to the blockchain 

Adds a new block to the blockchain. If the block\textquotesingle{}s parent is not the current top of the blockchain, the block may be added to an alternate chain. If the block does not belong, is already in the blockchain or an alternate chain, or is invalid, return false.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em bl} & the block to be added \\
\hline
{\em bvc} & metadata about the block addition\textquotesingle{}s success/failure \\
\hline
{\em checkpoint} & optional checkpoint if there is one associated with the block\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true on successful addition to the blockchain, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} cryptonote\+::\+Blockchain\+::check\+\_\+block\+\_\+timestamp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1block}{block}} \&}]{b }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a45843094159b666c3e9463e3b48e66e1}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a45843094159b666c3e9463e3b48e66e1}} 
\index{cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}!check\_block\_timestamp@{check\_block\_timestamp}}
\index{check\_block\_timestamp@{check\_block\_timestamp}!cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{check\_block\_timestamp()}{check\_block\_timestamp()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::check\+\_\+block\+\_\+timestamp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1block}{block}} \&}]{b,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t \&}]{median\+\_\+ts }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



checks a block\textquotesingle{}s timestamp 

This function grabs the timestamps from the most recent $<$n$>$ blocks, where n = B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+C\+H\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+S\+T\+A\+M\+P\+\_\+\+C\+H\+E\+C\+K\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+OW. If there are not those many blocks in the blockchain, the timestap is assumed to be valid. If there are, this function returns\+: true if the block\textquotesingle{}s timestamp is not less than the timestamp of the median of the selected blocks false otherwise


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em b} & the block to be checked \\
\hline
{\em median\+\_\+ts} & return-\/by-\/reference the median of timestamps\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the block\textquotesingle{}s timestamp is valid, otherwise false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

checks a block\textquotesingle{}s timestamp 

If the block is not more recent than the median of the recent timestamps passed here, it is considered invalid.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{check\_fee()}{check\_fee()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::check\+\_\+fee (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{tx\+\_\+weight,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{tx\+\_\+outs,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{fee,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{burned,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1tx__pool__options}{tx\+\_\+pool\+\_\+options}} \&}]{opts }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



validate a transaction\textquotesingle{}s fee 

This function validates the fee is enough for the transaction. This is based on the weight of the transaction, and, after a height threshold, on the average weight of transaction in a past window. From Loki v13 the amount must also include a per-\/output-\/created fee.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em tx\+\_\+weight} & the transaction weight \\
\hline
{\em tx\+\_\+outs} & the number of outputs created in the transaction \\
\hline
{\em fee} & the miner tx fee (any burned component must already be removed, such as is done by get\+\_\+tx\+\_\+miner\+\_\+fee) \\
\hline
{\em burned} & the amount of coin burned in this tx \\
\hline
{\em opts} & transaction pool options used to pass through required fee/burn amounts\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the fee is enough, false otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::check\+\_\+tx\+\_\+input (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1txin__to__key}{txin\+\_\+to\+\_\+key}} \&}]{txin,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1hash}{crypto\+::hash}} \&}]{tx\+\_\+prefix\+\_\+hash,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structrct_1_1ctkey}{rct\+::ctkey}} $>$ \&}]{output\+\_\+keys,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



collect output public keys of a transaction input set 

This function locates all outputs associated with a given input set (mixins) and validates that they exist and are usable (unlocked, unspent is checked elsewhere).

If pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height is not N\+U\+LL, its value is set to the height of the most recent block which contains an output used in the input set


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em txin} & the transaction input \\
\hline
{\em tx\+\_\+prefix\+\_\+hash} & the transaction prefix hash, for caching organization \\
\hline
{\em output\+\_\+keys} & return-\/by-\/reference the public keys of the outputs in the input set \\
\hline
{\em pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height} & return-\/by-\/pointer the height of the most recent block in the input set\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false if any output is not yet unlocked, or is missing, otherwise true 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{check\_tx\_inputs()}{check\_tx\_inputs()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} cryptonote\+::\+Blockchain\+::check\+\_\+tx\+\_\+inputs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcryptonote_1_1transaction}{transaction}} \&}]{tx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1tx__verification__context}{tx\+\_\+verification\+\_\+context}} \&}]{tvc,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pmax\+\_\+used\+\_\+block\+\_\+height = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{std\+::unordered\+\_\+set$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1key__image}{crypto\+::key\+\_\+image}} $>$ $\ast$}]{key\+\_\+image\+\_\+conflicts = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



validate a transaction\textquotesingle{}s inputs and their keys 

This function validates transaction inputs and their keys. Previously it also performed double spend checking, but that has been moved to its own function. The transaction\textquotesingle{}s rct signatures, if any, are expanded.

If pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height is not N\+U\+LL, its value is set to the height of the most recent block which contains an output used in any input set

Currently this function calls ring signature validation for each transaction.

This fails if called on a non-\/standard metadata transaction such as a deregister; you generally want to call check\+\_\+tx() instead, which calls this if appropriate.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em tx} & the transaction to validate \\
\hline
{\em tvc} & returned information about tx verification \\
\hline
{\em pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height} & return-\/by-\/pointer the height of the most recent block in the input set \\
\hline
{\em key\+\_\+image\+\_\+conflicts} & if specified then don\textquotesingle{}t fail on duplicate key images but instead add them here for the caller to decide on\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false if any validation step fails, otherwise true 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_afcca64964ff6585f4f70af9680557839}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_afcca64964ff6585f4f70af9680557839}}

validates a transaction\textquotesingle{}s inputs 

validates a transaction\textquotesingle{}s inputs as correctly used and not previously spent. also returns the hash and height of the most recent block which contains an output that was used as an input to the transaction. The transaction\textquotesingle{}s rct signatures, if any, are expanded.

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

false if any input is invalid, otherwise true

expands v2 transaction data from blockchain 

Ring\+CT transactions do not transmit some of their data if it can be reconstituted by the receiver. This function expands that implicit data. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a9167de9d55e7243beeef80129636a19a}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a9167de9d55e7243beeef80129636a19a}}

get recent block hashes for a foreign chain 

Find the split point between us and foreign blockchain and return (by reference) the most recent common block hash along with up to B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+S\+\_\+\+I\+D\+S\+\_\+\+S\+Y\+N\+C\+H\+R\+O\+N\+I\+Z\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+U\+NT additional (more recent) hashes.

\hline
{\em resp} & return-\/by-\/reference the split height and subsequent blocks\textquotesingle{} hashes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if a block found in common, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

find the most recent common point between ours and a foreign chain 

This function takes a list of block hashes from another node on the network to find where the split point is between us and them. This is used to see what to send another node that needs to sync.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if a block found in common, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

get recent blocks for a foreign chain 

This function gets recent blocks relative to a foreign chain, starting either at a requested height or whatever height is the most recent ours and the foreign chain have in common.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em req\+\_\+start\+\_\+block} & if non-\/zero, specifies a start point (otherwise find most recent commonality) \\
\hline
{\em qblock\+\_\+ids} & the foreign chain\textquotesingle{}s \char`\"{}short history\char`\"{} (see get\+\_\+short\+\_\+chain\+\_\+history) \\
\hline
{\em blocks} & return-\/by-\/reference the blocks and their transactions \\
\hline
{\em total\+\_\+height} & return-\/by-\/reference our current blockchain height \\
\hline
{\em start\+\_\+height} & return-\/by-\/reference the height of the first block returned \\
\hline
{\em pruned} & whether to return full or pruned tx blobs \\
\hline
{\em max\+\_\+count} & the max number of blocks to get\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if a block found in common or req\+\_\+start\+\_\+block specified, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecryptonote_af37f245483e045f6ffb814fa60271d20}{byte\+\_\+and\+\_\+output\+\_\+fees}} Blockchain\+::get\+\_\+dynamic\+\_\+base\+\_\+fee (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{block\+\_\+reward,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{median\+\_\+block\+\_\+weight,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecryptonote_a884c13f6c17c6ce8dd15f2e9bc4c75ef}{hf}}}]{version }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



get dynamic per-\/kB or -\/byte fee and the per-\/output fee for a given block weight and hard fork version. 

The dynamic per-\/byte fee is based on the block weight in a past window, and the current block reward. It is expressed as a per-\/kiB value before v8, and per byte from v8.

The per-\/output fee is a fixed amount per output created in the transaction beginning in Loki hard fork 13 and will be 0 before v13.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em block\+\_\+reward} & the current block reward \\
\hline
{\em median\+\_\+block\+\_\+weight} & the median block weight in the past window \\
\hline
{\em version} & hard fork version for rules and constants to use\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pair of \{per-\/size, per-\/output\} fees 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a4c7302b03882ca457bfa01e5e24f2c9f}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a4c7302b03882ca457bfa01e5e24f2c9f}}

\index{cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}!get\_short\_chain\_history@{get\_short\_chain\_history}}
\index{get\_short\_chain\_history@{get\_short\_chain\_history}!cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_short\_chain\_history()}{get\_short\_chain\_history()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Blockchain\+::get\+\_\+short\+\_\+chain\+\_\+history (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1hash}{crypto\+::hash}} $>$ \&}]{ids }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



gets the hashes for a sample of the blockchain 

Builds a list of hashes representing certain blocks from the blockchain in reverse chronological order for comparison of chains when synchronizing. The sampled blocks include the most recent blocks, then drops off exponentially back to the genesis block.

Specifically the blocks chosen for height H, are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item the most recent 11 (H-\/1, H-\/2, ..., H-\/10, H-\/11)
\item base-\/2 exponential drop off from there, so\+: H-\/13, H-\/17, H-\/25, etc... (going down to, at smallest, height 1)
\item the genesis block (height 0) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a214928ef554dcf2af71a7809609b0a46}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_a214928ef554dcf2af71a7809609b0a46}} 
\index{cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}!get\_split\_transactions\_blobs@{get\_split\_transactions\_blobs}}

\index{cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}!have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent@{have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent}}
\index{have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent@{have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent}!cryptonote::Blockchain@{cryptonote::Blockchain}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent()}{have\_tx\_keyimg\_as\_spent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::have\+\_\+tx\+\_\+keyimg\+\_\+as\+\_\+spent (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1key__image}{crypto\+::key\+\_\+image}} \&}]{key\+\_\+im }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



check if a key image is already spent on the blockchain 

Whenever a transaction output is used as an input for another transaction (a true input, not just one of a mixing set), a key image is generated and stored in the transaction in order to prevent double spending. If this key image is seen again, the transaction using it is rejected.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em key\+\_\+im} & the key image to search for\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the key image is already spent in the blockchain, else false 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_ad025b9550f2771e1ed3ae5ac5eff986e}\label{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain_ad025b9550f2771e1ed3ae5ac5eff986e}}

reverts the blockchain to its previous state following a failed switch 

If \mbox{\hyperlink{classcryptonote_1_1Blockchain}{Blockchain}} fails to switch to an alternate chain when it means to do so, this function reverts the blockchain to how it was before the attempted switch.

{\em rollback\+\_\+height} & the height to revert to before appending the original chain\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$class visitor\+\_\+t $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::scan\+\_\+outputkeys\+\_\+for\+\_\+indexes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1txin__to__key}{txin\+\_\+to\+\_\+key}} \&}]{tx\+\_\+in\+\_\+to\+\_\+key,  }\item[{visitor\+\_\+t \&}]{vis,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1hash}{crypto\+::hash}} \&}]{tx\+\_\+prefix\+\_\+hash,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height = {\ttfamily NULL} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



collects the keys for all outputs being \char`\"{}spent\char`\"{} as an input 

This function makes sure that each \char`\"{}input\char`\"{} in an input (mixins) exists and collects the public key for each from the transaction it was included in via the visitor passed to it.

If pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height is not N\+U\+LL, its value is set to the height of the most recent block which contains an output used in the input set


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em visitor\+\_\+t} & a class encapsulating tx is unlocked and collect tx key \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em tx\+\_\+in\+\_\+to\+\_\+key} & a transaction input instance \\
\hline
{\em vis} & an instance of the visitor to use \\
\hline
{\em tx\+\_\+prefix\+\_\+hash} & the hash of the associated \mbox{\hyperlink{classcryptonote_1_1transaction__prefix}{transaction\+\_\+prefix}} \\
\hline
{\em pmax\+\_\+related\+\_\+block\+\_\+height} & return-\/by-\/pointer the height of the most recent block in the input set \\
\hline
{\em tx\+\_\+version} & version of the tx, if $>$ 1 we also get commitments\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false if any keys are not found or any inputs are not unlocked, otherwise true 
\end{DoxyReturn}

performs a blockchain reorganization according to the longest chain rule 

This function aggregates all the actions necessary to switch to a newly-\/longer chain. If any step in the reorganization process fails, the blockchain is reverted to its previous state.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em alt\+\_\+chain} & the chain to switch to \\
\hline
{\em keep\+\_\+disconnected\+\_\+chain} & whether or not to keep the old chain as an alternate\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false if the reorganization fails, otherwise true 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em long\+\_\+term\+\_\+effective\+\_\+median\+\_\+block\+\_\+weight} & optionally return that value\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{stdbool_8h_a1062901a7428fdd9c7f180f5e01ea056}{bool}} Blockchain\+::validate\+\_\+miner\+\_\+transaction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structcryptonote_1_1block}{block}} \&}]{b,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{cumulative\+\_\+block\+\_\+weight,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{fee,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t \&}]{base\+\_\+reward,  }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{already\+\_\+generated\+\_\+coins,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacecryptonote_a884c13f6c17c6ce8dd15f2e9bc4c75ef}{hf}}}]{version }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}



validates a miner (coinbase) transaction 

This function makes sure that the miner calculated his reward correctly and that his miner transaction totals reward + fee.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em b} & the block containing the miner transaction to be validated \\
\hline
{\em cumulative\+\_\+block\+\_\+weight} & the block\textquotesingle{}s weight \\
\hline
{\em fee} & the total fees collected in the block \\
\hline
{\em base\+\_\+reward} & return-\/by-\/reference the new block\textquotesingle{}s generated coins \\
\hline
{\em already\+\_\+generated\+\_\+coins} & the amount of currency generated prior to this block \\
\hline
{\em version} & hard fork version for that transaction\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
false if anything is found wrong with the miner transaction, otherwise true 
\end{DoxyReturn}
